# X

[Back to index](index.md)

## xab

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `XAB`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to trade, exchange, or transfer reciprocally
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** law-governance, economics-provision, travel-place
- **Root family:** `XB`; Law/civic life; trade, exchange, market transfer; trade, exchange, market, reciprocal transfer
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** X-B root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na xab.
- **Corpus:** observed (2 attestations); tracks: literary-poetic; examples in poetic-096

## xab-da

- **Pronunciation:** `XAPAR-GA`
- **Part of speech:** noun
- **Definition:** ongoing process, practice, or craft of: to gain expertise, train knowing, or judge by practiced skill
- **Register/status:** technical; accepted
- **Domains:** science-math, philosophy-metaphysics, emotion-psychology
- **Root family:** `XPR`; Seeing/knowing; expertise, trained knowing; expertise, trained knowing, disciplined competence
- **Pattern:** process
- **Literal:** X-P-R root, process suffix -ga
- **Example:** Xapar-ga ga ban rih.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)
